NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

[Part VI—Sec. 4

NOTICE
Resolution of Voluntary Winding up
In the matter of Companies Act, 1956
and
Polymatech Trading India Private Limited registered on 29th July 2009.
At the Extraordinary General meeting of the above named company held at Door No. 21, (Old No. 11),
Ground Floor-1, Sri Krishna Kutira Apartments, Harrington Road, Chetpet, Chennai-600 031, Tamil Nadu on September
22, 2011 the following resolution was passed:
Special Resolution:
“RESOLVED THAT pursuant to Section 484(1)(b) of the Companies Act, 1956, the Company be wound up voluntarily.”
“RESOLVED FURTHER THAT any one of the Directors of the Company be and is hereby severally authorised to do
all such acts, deeds and things, sign such documents as may be necessary to give effect to the aforesaid resolution
including signing and filing of the necessary forms and documents with the Registrar of Companies, Chennai, Tamil Nadu.”
For Crest Law Partners
RAVITEJ RAO, M,
Liquidator.

Chennai,
22nd, September 2011.

FORM No. 151
(See rule 315)
COMPANIES ACT, 1956
MEMBERS’ VOLUNTARY WINDING UP
Polymatech Trading India Private Limited registered on 29th July 2009.

Name of the Company

Polymatech Trading India Private Limited

Date of Incorporation of the Company

29th July 2009

Nature of Business

various industrial equipments.
